2063<h1>

206410 Modern Kitchen Ideas for a Sleek, Cutting-Edge Design</h1>

2065

2066</div>

2067</div>

2068</div>

2069</div>

2070<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cfa-feb--be-fcbeb">

2073<div>

2074<h6>

2075November 11, 2021</h6>

2076

2077

2078<h6>

2079Mikael Short</h6>

2080

2081</div>

2082</div>

2083</div>

2084</div>

2085</div>

2095<div class="">

2096<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ba-eee-c-bf-dae">

2097<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ba-eee-c-bf-dae">

2100<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

2102<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-eca--f-ac-ba">

2103<div class="merce-column-container">

2104<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-aed--f-a-faadad">

2105<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf aed--f-a-faadad-singleImageAlignment">

2106<a href="https://vevano.com/page/shop-faucets/">

2107<img class="aed--f-a-faadad-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/-YCjb8J0cUWsjdgUMQQvDbwAD1g8jFVjRfCnFtcxO_8/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL0Jhbm5lcnMvYmxkZWFsMTVmYXVjZXRzbW9iaWxlLnBuZw" alt="15% off Faucet Orders Over $200. Use code BLDEAL15 at checkout." title="15% off Faucet Orders Over $200. Use code BLDEAL15 at checkout."/>

2108</a>

2110</div>

2111</div>

2112</div>

2113</div>

2114</div>

2115</div>

2116</div>

2117</div>

2118</div>

2119</div>

2120</div>

2121<div class="">

2122<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-dab-da-c-ac-cea">

2123<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-dab-da-c-ac-cea">

2124<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

2125<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

2126<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

2127<div class="">

2128<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-aac-ad-e-b-ebbec">

2129<div class="merce-column-container">

2130<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-d--e-e-bdba">

2131<div>

2132<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2133<div>

2134<p>

2135When it comes to designing a modern kitchen design, the motto is form follows function. In other words, the shape of the object should relate to the purpose it serves. In modern designs, everything should serve a purpose, and what better place to optimize function and style than the busy hub of your kitchen?</p>

2136

2137

2138<p>

2139The standard modern aesthetic is sleek and minimalistic in nature, with clean, straight lines throughout and open areas. Modern kitchens are known for uncluttered, functional spaciousness. The openness is used just as much as any decor, and everything has its place to minimize clutter.</p>

2140

2141</div>

2142</div>

2143</div>

2144</div>

2145<div class="Layout-module_hidden-xs__2UQIp Layout-module_visible-sm__Z2eD8 Layout-module_visible-md__1t5sZ Layout-module_visible-lg__1PfV6 visibility-plugin-wrapper">

2146<div class="">

2147<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-af-ac-e-ab-ea">

2148<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-af-ac-e-ab-ea">

2150<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

2151<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

2152<div class="">

2153<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-cfa-bc-a-ce-dba">

2154<div class="merce-column-container">

2179<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2180<div>

2181<p>

2182<em>

2183<span style="font-size:18px;">

2184&ldquo;Modernistic style really comes down to two things: simplicity and functionality. Make sure everything has a purpose.&rdquo; &nbsp;</span>

2185</em>

2186<strong>

2187&mdash;Martha McNamara</strong>

2188</p>

2189

2190</div>

2191</div>

2193</div>

2194<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-ef-ec--bd-dcf">

2195<div class="">

2196<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2197</div>

2198</div>

2199<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bc-da--d-ebd">

2200<div>

2201<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2202<div>

2203<p>

2204While modern style has been around for some time, it&rsquo;s seeing a resurgence in popularity, especially since hybrid styles lean on the clean lines and functionality the modern style brings. The kitchen is also a prime place to allow the modern style to highlight beautiful sleek designs and optimal functionality.</p>

2205

2213<div>

2214<h2>

2215What is Modern Kitchen Design?</h2>

2216

2217</div>

2218</div>

2219</div>

2220</div>

2224</div>

2225</div>

2226<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-baab-b-ad-ab-edba">

2227<div>

2228<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2229<div>

2230<p>

2231The beauty of <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-style-modern-design/" target="_blank">

2232modern design</a>

2233 lies in its functional simplicity: straight lines, neutral colors, and uncluttered surfaces and textures. These features are easily translated into a kitchen.</p>

2234

2235

2236<p>

2237Open spaces are also a signature of modern designs. Relying on natural lighting from windows contributes to that spacious feel in a modern kitchen.</p>

2238

2239</div>

2240</div>

2241</div>

2242</div>

2243<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-aacb-e---dbd">

2244<div class="">

2245<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2246</div>

2247</div>

2248<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ccdbd-b--d-cfdce">

2249<div>

2250<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2251<div>

2252<p>

2253<em>

2254<span style="font-size:18px;">

2255&ldquo;Natural light is key to achieving a modern interior style. Windows open up the room and help to provide those essential vertical and horizontal lines.&rdquo;</span>

2256</em>

2257&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>

2258&mdash;Martha McNamara, Vevano Director of Product and Design</strong>

2259</p>

2260

2261</div>

2262</div>

2263</div>

2264</div>

2265<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-a-cba-be-bc-b">

2266<div class="">

2267<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2268</div>

2269</div>

2270<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aea-d-a-b-fbb">

2271<div>

2272<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2273<div>

2274<p>

2275The primary shapes in a modern kitchen are straight lines, whether vertical or horizontal. You can create this effect with simple, streamlined cabinet designs, solid yet neutral colors, or simple linear patterns.</p>

2276

2277

2278<p>

2279The point in modern design is that everything serves a purpose and everything has its place. Another popular descriptor is raison d&rsquo;&ecirc;tre, which means &ldquo;reason to be&rdquo; in French. No clutter means cleaner lines to emphasize a modern aesthetic.</p>

2280

2281

2282<p>

2283Like <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-styles-minimalist-design/" target="_blank">

2284minimalist designs</a>

2285, which are a bit more extreme and stark, modern designs take inspiration from Scandinavian design styles where style follows function. Less is more when it comes to modern design.</p>

2286

2287</div>

2288</div>

2289</div>

2290</div>

2295<h3>

2296Modern Kitchen Color Palette</h3>

2297

2298</div>

2299</div>

2300</div>

2301</div>

2302<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-cbd-e-e-ce-cfffeda">

2309<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2310<div>

2311<p>

2312The colors that make up a modern kitchen design are primarily neutral with bold splashes or pops of color. The colors you&rsquo;ll most often find in a modern kitchen are whites, blacks, grays, and other neutral or even natural tones, like light wood.</p>

2313

2314

2315<p>

2316In terms of accent colors to draw the eye, bold colors are welcome in small amounts in modern design, such as bright primary colors like red, blue, and yellow.</p>

2317

2318</div>

2319</div>

2332<em>

2333<span style="font-size:18px;">

2334&ldquo;When it comes to colors, neutral tones should take priority, followed by shades of white, then black. Embrace natural elements such as wood grain and leather.&rdquo;</span>

2335</em>

2336&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>

2337&ndash; Martha McNamara</strong>

2338</p>

2353<h3>

2354Modern Kitchen Finishes</h3>

2355

2356</div>

2357</div>

2358</div>

2359</div>

2360<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-dcfc-abb-b-cf-dd">

2361<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf dcfc-abb-b-cf-dd-singleImageAlignment">

2362<img class="dcfc-abb-b-cf-dd-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/DZT5b0EvrFu8z1ZvFQlRq-fW1sX2D1raadYVAAZrAwU/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbWFrZS15b3VyLWtpdGNoZW4tbW9kZXJuLTQuanBn" alt="modern black kitchen sink" title="modern black kitchen sink"/>

2363</div>

2364</div>

2365<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cdc---b-b">

2366<div>

2367<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2368<div>

2369<p>

2370Modern takes pieces from both natural and industrial to enhance its form-follows-function design.</p>

2371

2372

2373<p>

2374Modern finishes for your kitchen might include chrome, steel, glass, and even wood. Reflective surfaces and fixtures are perfect for reflecting modern stylings. Whereas, if you&rsquo;re craving a bit more warmth in your modern kitchen, wood-look and wood colors can help to soften up the room too.</p>

2375

2376

2377<p>

2378Pairing steel fixtures and elements with wood is not unheard of in modern styles. Leather could also be a complementary texture in a modern kitchen, especially in upholstery like dining chairs or stools.</p>

2379

2387<div>

2388<h3>

2389When Modern Becomes More</h3>

2390

2391</div>

2392</div>

2393</div>

2394</div>

2395<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-cbff-cf--cd-a">

2396<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf cbff-cf--cd-a-singleImageAlignment">

2397<img class="cbff-cf--cd-a-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/TxYtprl1co20m-EMqH406mBvzGEgO--kVzbw28ZbswA/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL2hleGFnb24tYmFja3NwbGFzaC1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi5qcGc" alt="modern farmhouse kitchen" title="modern farmhouse kitchen"/>

2398</div>

2399</div>

2400<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ce--f-ba-ef">

2401<div>

2402<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2403<div>

2404<p>

2405Modern design is often incorporated into other kitchen design types thanks to its simple and sleek appearance, clean lines, and functionality. For example, the <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/modern-farmhouse-kitchen-design-ideas/" target="_blank">

2406modern farmhouse kitchen</a>

2407 is also a very popular design style for its beautiful simplicity with warmer decorative touches. And mid-century modern harkens back to modern&rsquo;s clean lines and functionality but with more variety in shapes and contrasting natural materials.</p>

2408

2409

2410<p>

2411Know that modern style is different from contemporary style, even if both modern and contemporary mean the same thing in the dictionary. <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-styles-contemporary-design/" target="_blank">

2412Contemporary styles</a>

2413 rely on what designs are trending at the moment and change with the times. In contrast, the modern style has a distinct look and function that emerged in the 1930s with clean lines, a neutral color palette, and utility as a priority.</p>

2414

2415</div>

2416</div>

2417</div>

2418</div>

2419<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fd--aa-ba-cb">

2420<div>

2421<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2422<div>

2423<h2>

242410 Ideas to Make Your Kitchen More Modern</h2>

2425

2426

2427<p>

2428The sleek and minimalist modern vibe is popular to create a clean and clear kitchen to work from. You can absolutely achieve a modern style in your kitchen through minor renovations.</p>

2429

2430

2431<p>

2432In modern styles, furniture and d&eacute;cor should be both beautiful and purposeful in design and placement. The key is that you should only see the cabinets and the countertops. Vevano Home Designer Michael says, &ldquo;You shouldn&rsquo;t see very much stuff.&rdquo;</p>

2433

2434

2435<p>

2436If you&rsquo;re looking to update your outdated kitchen, here are ten modern kitchen design ideas to transform your kitchen with a minimalistic yet functional modern flair.</p>

2437

2438

2439<h3>

24401. Opt for Minimally Designed Cabinets</h3>

2441

2442</div>

2443</div>

2444</div>

2445</div>

2446<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-bdd--a-ec-fadc">

2447<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf bdd--a-ec-fadc-singleImageAlignment">

2448<img class="bdd--a-ec-fadc-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/HmBhaM2GZ-dXSad9goOnRzCeYBQ3vGXrlLuCcFK0qys/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbWFrZS15b3VyLWtpdGNoZW4tbW9kZXJuLTMuanBn" alt="modern white kitchen cabinets" title="modern white kitchen cabinets"/>

2449</div>

2450</div>

2451<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-c-ffa-e-d-ddae">

2452<div>

2453<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2454<div>

2455<p>

2456<a href="https://vevano.com/page/modern-kitchen-cabinets/" target="_blank">

2457Modern kitchen cabinets</a>

2458 are simple in style yet highly functional. They often lack ornamentation or other decorative features, opting for streamlined and straightforward styles.</p>

2459

2460

2461<p>

2462Slab-style frameless doors are the most popular modern <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-door-styles-101/" target="_blank">

2463cabinet door style</a>

2464. If you don&rsquo;t want to replace your cabinets entirely, you can always replace just the doors to achieve the modern style you want.</p>

2465

2466

2467<p>

2468Modern kitchens will highlight cabinets in neutral colors, if not white or gray tones. White gloss cabinets, in particular, are quite popular in modern kitchen designs, though matte white also fits in.</p>

2469

2470

2471<p>

2472Contrasting the colors of your cabinets with floors, wall paint, and d&eacute;cor is another great way to add modern flair to the main hub of your home. Some ideas to add contrasting modern flair might be to pair white cabinets with a <a href="https://vevano.com/page/blue-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

2473navy blue kitchen cabinet</a>

2474 island or dark gray or <a href="https://vevano.com/page/black-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

2475black cabinets</a>

2476 with a white countertop. Using the contrast of light and dark colors is a modern technique to draw attention or intrigue in a monochromatic kitchen.</p>

2477

2478

2479<p>

2480Another way to add modern flair to your kitchen cabinets is to consider cabinets that function in unconventional ways that still offer functionality. Some modern cabinets open up rather from left to right!</p>

2481

2482</div>

2483</div>

2484</div>

2485</div>

2486<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-dec---ad-eaac">

2487<div class="">

2488<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2489</div>

2490</div>

2491<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-dd--e-c-bddc">

2492<div>

2493<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2494<div>

2495<p>

2496<em>

2497<span style="font-size:18px;">

2498&ldquo;Instead of upper cabinets that open with hinges, you could have flip-up door cabinets&mdash;something that shows you&rsquo;re thinking outside of the box. You can take normal, standard designs and make them even more functional.&rdquo; &nbsp;</span>

2499</em>

2500<strong>

2501&mdash;Madi, Vevano Home Designer</strong>

2502</p>

2503

2504</div>

2505</div>

2506</div>

2507</div>

2508<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-fbf-bf--adc-caefaeade">

2509<div class="">

2510<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2511</div>

2512</div>

2513<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ecf--c-fca-acb">

2514<div>

2515<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2516<div>

2517<p>

2518Less is more with modern cabinets, so select a collection without recessed or raised panels. We have various frameless cabinets that work well with a modern design style, as they have clean, straight lines.</p>

2519

2520

2521<p>

2522Form and function are essential in modern cabinetry so select base cabinets with rollout shelves or hidden trash compartments to maximize space and add convenience.</p>

2523

2524</div>

2525</div>

2526</div>

2527</div>

2528<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ff-a-cb-b-edf">

2529<div>

2532<h3>

25332. Ramp Up Your Cabinet Organization</h3>

2534

2535</div>

2536</div>

2537</div>

2538</div>

2539<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-dea-ef-a-d-ffbcc">

2540<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf dea-ef-a-d-ffbcc-singleImageAlignment">

2541<img class="dea-ef-a-d-ffbcc-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/FQ0-bEOUEc7zL6ggJdRaVdXKDbYqg6TKNf5wr7BNwHM/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbW9kZXJuLWtpdGNoZW4tY2FiaW5ldC1vcmdhbml6YXRpb24uanBn" alt="modern wooden cabinet organization" title="modern wooden cabinet organization"/>

2542</div>

2543</div>

2544<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ffdb--dda-a-eadc">

2545<div>

2546<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2547<div>

2548<p>

2549Even if you don&rsquo;t see the functionality through the minimalistic modern design, the sleek exterior of modern cabinets could open to reveal a host of organizational tools that maximize the space in your cabinets.</p>

2550

2551

2552<p>

2553You can strategically organize your cabinet and drawer space with lazy-susans, pull-out shelves (like a <a href="https://vevano.com/product/7017-432-wf42-3c-432-series-natural-maple-between-cabinet-pull-out-organizer-3-x-112-x-42/" target="_blank">

2554between-cabinet pull-out organizer</a>

2555), <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/how-to-organize-spices" target="_blank">

2556spice organizers</a>

2557, <a href="https://vevano.com/product/40679-5psp-15sc-cr-5psp-series-chrome-blind-corner-optimizer-with-soft-close-2625-x-2025-x-21/" target="_blank">

2558blind corner optimizers</a>

2559, and so much more. To make your heavy items stored in cabinets easier to access, <a href="https://vevano.com/product/7094-ml-mphdsccr-18-ml-series-natural-maple-base-cabinet-appliance-lift-shelf-1175-x-20-x-138/" target="_blank">

2560base cabinet appliance lifts</a>

2561 are also available.</p>

2562

2563

2564<p>

2565In-cabinet storage space will allow for clear countertop space and clean lines to prevail in your kitchen. Give your cabinets a modern upgrade with utility to spare with such cabinet organizers.</p>

2566

2567

2568<p>

2569Nowadays, a wide variety of <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/how-to-organize-kitchen-cabinets/" target="_blank">

2570cabinet organization ideas</a>

2571 and tools are available to keep your cooking tools out of sight but ready to pull out!</p>

2580<div>

2581<h3>

25823. Brush Up Your Hardware</h3>

2583

2584</div>

2585</div>

2586</div>

2587</div>

2588<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ad-ad-a-add-eec">

2589<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ad-ad-a-add-eec-singleImageAlignment">

2590<img class="ad-ad-a-add-eec-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/eHzVB5Vo5l5pe8mwp_5Ab4UVq4xTAXDIeNRcQLTD9-I/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbWFrZS15b3VyLWtpdGNoZW4tbW9kZXJuLTEuanBn" alt="modern kitchen silver hardware" title="modern kitchen silver hardware"/>

2591</div>

2592</div>

2593<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cabaddb-d---fd">

2594<div>

2595<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2596<div>

2597<p>

2598Replacing the hardware in your kitchen is a quick and easy way to modernize your kitchen.</p>

2599

2600

2601<p>

2602Pulls and knobs are welcome in modern styles, though pulls are a more popular choice. Handles that lean industrial or farmhouse in style may also work well in a modern kitchen. Look for straight, angular lines to match the modern theme.</p>

2603

2604

2605<p>

2606Hardware with too much ornamentation or swirling decorations may look out of place in a modern kitchen unless you&rsquo;re going for a modern farmhouse look.</p>

2607

2608

2609<p>

2610Chrome and steel, as well as other metals, are mainstay hardware finishes in modern styles. Textures such as brushed, polished, matte, or satin are also very popular with modern kitchen cabinet designs.</p>

2611

2612

2613<p>

2614Easy-to-grab pulls with simple designs are best for continuing the pure-modern aesthetic of your kitchen.</p>

2615

2616</div>

2617</div>

2618</div>

2619</div>

2620<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ae-ae-eff-a-bd">

2621<div>

2622<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2623<div>

2624<h3>

26254. Lighting for Function</h3>

2626

2627</div>

2628</div>

2629</div>

2630</div>

2631<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ccca-c-ca--daaf">

2632<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ccca-c-ca--daaf-singleImageAlignment">

2633<img class="ccca-c-ca--daaf-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/T-oLnCyKuDlLTpym7Id62WiigGeQMwSDmOVge8qCWO8/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbWFrZS15b3VyLWtpdGNoZW4tbW9kZXJuLTcuanBn" alt="modern kitchen natural lighting" title="modern kitchen natural lighting"/>

2634</div>

2635</div>

2636<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cffc-ca-a-fd-deddae">

2637<div>

2638<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2639<div>

2640<p>

2641Use as much natural light as possible before you add in other light fixtures. Natural light from windows will open up a room and make it look bigger. Square or rectangle windows will work well in a modern kitchen, thanks to their straight lines.</p>

2642

2643

2644<p>

2645From there, use lighting for functional purposes, such as under-cabinet task lighting or a pendant light over the kitchen island.</p>

2646

2647

2648<p>

2649Ideal finishes for modern lighting fixtures include metals, glass, and wood.</p>

2650

2651

2652<p>

2653A statement lighting piece is a great way to add your personality to the sleek modern style. One way to make your lighting fixture pop would be to maintain a matte black finish on the rest of your kitchen hardware and then using a gold finish on your lighting fixture.</p>

2654

2655</div>

2656</div>

2657</div>

2658</div>

2659<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-dc-d-e--efadee">

2660<div class="">

2661<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2662</div>

2663</div>

2664<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-afee-d---becbd">

2665<div>

2666<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2667<div>

2668<p>

2669<em>

2670<span style="font-size:18px;">

2671&ldquo;You could have a super sleek, minimalistic kitchen but a very expensive light fixture or elaborate island. You can channel your expenses into a statement piece to make it pop in your modern kitchen.&rdquo;</span>

2672</em>

2673&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>

2674&mdash;Michael, Vevano Home Designer</strong>

2675</p>

2676

2677</div>

2678</div>

2679</div>

2680</div>

2681<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-dad-afe-e-e-eeae">

2682<div class="">

2683<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2684</div>

2685</div>

2686<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-baea-fd-b-a-bdbbcda">

2687<div>

2688<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2689<div>

2690<p>

2691In terms of what to avoid in lighting to stay modern, our designers recommend avoiding lanterns or crystal chandeliers that would come across as too traditional.</p>

2692

2693</div>

2694</div>

2695</div>

2696</div>

2697<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fdae-b-cb-f-aacfefe">

2698<div>

2699<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2700<div>

2701<h3>

27025. Clear Countertops</h3>

2703

2704</div>

2705</div>

2706</div>

2707</div>

2708<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-fb--f-ab-bddfcea">

2709<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf fb--f-ab-bddfcea-singleImageAlignment">

2710<img class="fb--f-ab-bddfcea-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/AkjKN0-TLCwofUr_WmZnnlM1uAr3ul_7GIXRGDBKt7Q/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbWFrZS15b3VyLWtpdGNoZW4tbW9kZXJuLTguanBn" alt="modern clean kitchen countertop" title="modern clean kitchen countertop"/>

2711</div>

2712</div>

2713<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fafa-bb-cee-aaf-fdf">

2714<div>

2715<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2716<div>

2717<p>

2718The idea of a modern countertop is simple&mdash;keep it clear and clean.</p>

2719

2720

2721<p>

2722Quartz or marble would be welcome materials in a modern kitchen, particularly engineered quartz countertops.</p>

2723

2724

2725<p>

2726When it comes to color, select countertops with neutral tones to enhance your modern kitchen. Anything too bold in color or overly veiny doesn&rsquo;t necessarily fit the neutral modern color scheme.</p>

2727

2728

2729<p>

2730For a dramatic modern contrast, Vevano Home designers say that black quartz with white veining countertop would pop deliciously among <a href="https://vevano.com/page/white-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

2731white cabinets</a>

2732.</p>

2733

2734</div>

2735</div>

2736</div>

2737</div>

2738<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cb-d-edf-c-dcc">

2739<div>

2740<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2741<div>

2742<h3>

27436. Find Your Faucet &amp; Sink</h3>

2744

2745</div>

2746</div>

2747</div>

2748</div>

2749<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ddff-e--b-cec">

2750<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ddff-e--b-cec-singleImageAlignment">

2751<img class="ddff-e--b-cec-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/qr_RDTmBwaFoXyIUGA_S3R-8WGA1FaWqywdu20cy1m4/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbWFrZS15b3VyLWtpdGNoZW4tbW9kZXJuLTUuanBn" alt="modern kitchen sink" title="modern kitchen sink"/>

2752</div>

2753</div>

2754<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ae-ff-ba-df-addea">

2755<div>

2756<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2757<div>

2758<p>

2759Minimalistic styles and simple shapes for faucets and sinks are ideal for a modern kitchen.</p>

2760

2761

2762<p>

2763Our designers recommend a sleek pull-down faucet to fit a modern sink, such as the <a href="https://vevano.com/product/22116-lg529-esab-stellen-touchless-pull-down-kitchen-faucet-in-matte-black/" target="_blank">

2764touch-less pull-down faucet</a>

2765 in matte black.</p>

2766

2767

2768<p>

2769Undermount sinks are &ldquo;the way to go,&rdquo; as our designers suggest maintaining clean lines from the countertop into the basin. Stainless steel works great for functionality and for a modern sink material.</p>

2770

2771

2772<p>

2773Our designers recommend avoiding farmhouse sinks and drop-in sinks since they don&rsquo;t provide clean, straight lines inherent in modern styles, and they may be more fitting for traditional or farmhouse style kitchens.</p>

2774

2775

2776<p>

2777Since functionality is king, you can optimize your sink area with cutting boards and other integrated accessories. Look for sleek, minimal <a href="https://vevano.com/product/33510-cux16021-w-culinary-center-stainless-steel-double-basin-undermount-kitchen-sink/" target="_blank">

2778sink accessories </a>

2779so your sink doesn&rsquo;t look too cluttered.</p>

2780

2781</div>

2782</div>

2783</div>

2784</div>

2785<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ecc-eb-b-bce-eecf">

2786<div>

2787<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2788<div>

2789<h3>

27907. Back It Up with Backsplash</h3>

2791

2792</div>

2793</div>

2794</div>

2795</div>

2796<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-cfd-b-e-ab-bdcfd">

2797<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf cfd-b-e-ab-bdcfd-singleImageAlignment">

2798<img class="cfd-b-e-ab-bdcfd-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/eQ23QrR-Wl-HI_ot1qtj4jejwWaHlmkbPuLWNw_75nk/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbW9kZXJuLWtpdGNoZW4tYmFja3NwYXNoLTkuanBn" alt="modern kitchen hexagon backsplash " title="modern kitchen hexagon backsplash "/>

2799</div>

2800</div>

2801<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-e-eb-a--efae">

2802<div>

2803<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2804<div>

2805<p>

2806Some people like to use a backsplash to add a pop of color to their kitchen. For a modern kitchen, it&rsquo;s better to keep backsplash tiles neutral in color and simple in shape.</p>

2807

2808

2809<p>

2810Vevano Home designers recommend hexagonal tiles or a linear glass tile for backsplash in a modern kitchen. Another idea would be to extend the <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/types-of-countertops/" target="_blank">

2811countertop material</a>

2812 up the walls to keep the design uniform.</p>

2813

2814

2815<p>

2816While subway tiles could be used in a modern kitchen, our designers say they may suit other styles better, such as contemporary or farmhouse.</p>

2817

2818</div>

2819</div>

2820</div>

2821</div>

2822<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aac-e-ead-ac-dcaccecc">

2823<div>

2824<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2825<div>

2826<h3>

28278. Neutral Floors for Focus</h3>

2828

2829</div>

2830</div>

2831</div>

2832</div>

2833<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ba-da-b--ed">

2834<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ba-da-b--ed-singleImageAlignment">

2835<img class="ba-da-b--ed-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/MkJJxxQ70JnVnZs3dKSwVsbwZigiTZ2ezMVc1WvDTWA/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbWFrZS15b3VyLWtpdGNoZW4tbW9kZXJuLTYuanBn" alt="modern neutral kitchen flooring" title="modern neutral kitchen flooring"/>

2836</div>

2837</div>

2838<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fbfce--c-bb-e">

2839<div>

2840<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2841<div>

2842<p>

2843In a modern kitchen, it&rsquo;s unlikely your floor will be a statement piece. A neutral-toned floor would best underscore a modern kitchen to allow other focal points to draw your attention. Whites, light grays, or black floors would be ideal in a modern kitchen.</p>

2844

2845

2846<p>

2847Natural elements or colors work well as modern floors, particularly natural wood tones, which can be achieved through luxury vinyl tile (LVT) or tile. Light wood would also feature well as a flooring color in a modern kitchen since it&rsquo;s neutral enough in tone to fit in the modern color scheme.</p>

2848

2849</div>

2850</div>

2851</div>

2852</div>

2853<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bf-ad-e-fa-badba">

2854<div>

2855<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2856<div>

2857<h3>

28589. Strategic Deco Art</h3>

2859

2860</div>

2861</div>

2862</div>

2863</div>

2864<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-edd-bdf--ad-fccfcda">

2865<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf edd-bdf--ad-fccfcda-singleImageAlignment">

2866<img class="edd-bdf--ad-fccfcda-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/HehqH89lpVoJLEzZnLvH37GxNgYUGyK33pESPUfPDHk/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vbW9kZXJuLWtpdGNoZW4tYXJ0d29yay5qcGc" alt="modern kitchen artwork" title="modern kitchen artwork"/>

2867</div>

2868</div>

2869<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-e-d-b-bd-ecaed">

2870<div>

2871<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2872<div>

2873<p>

2874Artwork is one of the preferred ways to add a small pop of color to a modern kitchen.</p>

2875

2876

2877<p>

2878Deco art that fits within the modern style would be one to three art pieces featured on the walls, such as abstract art or a short photo series.</p>

2879

2880

2881<p>

2882Stick to simple frames or frameless art pieces to keep with the modern theme. Similarly, it&rsquo;s best to avoid art with added ornamentation or complex detailing.</p>

2883

2884</div>

2885</div>

2886</div>

2887</div>

2888<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-bbd--c-d-dadcb">

2889<div class="">

2890<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2891</div>

2892</div>

2893<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-c-cd-d-bbfb-baac">

2894<div>

2895<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2896<div>

2897<p>

2898<em>

2899<span style="font-size:18px;">

2900&ldquo;Instead of the whole canvas being colorful, choose a mostly gray or neutral-colored art piece with a stripe or pop of color.&rdquo;</span>

2901</em>

2902&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>

2903&mdash;Michael, Vevano Home Designer</strong>

2904</p>

2905

2906</div>

2907</div>

2908</div>

2909</div>

2910<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SEPARATOR-bdbc-ad-cf-a-bccfe">

2911<div class="">

2912<hr style="border-top:1px solid #ccc"/>

2913</div>

2914</div>

2915<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cdbbe-cc-e-ab-eceefe">

2916<div>

2917<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2918<div>

2919<h3>

292010. Clear Up Your Windows</h3>

2921

2922</div>

2923</div>

2924</div>

2925</div>

2926<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-bcb---bfc-cbab">

2927<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf bcb---bfc-cbab-singleImageAlignment">

2928<img class="bcb---bfc-cbab-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/oQ4GjR5uBra7-crfoUtQ7NfU8Dme4ikeLo2y0IVGGY0/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tYWtlLXlvdXIta2l0Y2hlbi1tb2Rlcm4vYmFubmVyLW1ha2UteW91ci1raXRjaGVuLW1vZGVybi5qcGc" alt="grey modern kitchen windows" title="grey modern kitchen windows"/>

2929</div>

2930</div>

2931<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bee-fc-e-bf-dbf">

2932<div>

2933<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2934<div>

2935<p>

2936Natural light from windows helps contribute to an open space that is befitting a modern kitchen. To maintain a modern aesthetic, keep your window treatments like curtains and shades minimal, if not simple and streamlined.</p>

2937

2938

2939<p>

2940Focus on highlighting clean and straight lines from your windows to optimize the light and make the kitchen feel more spacious.</p>

2941

2942

2943<h2>

2944In the end&hellip; A modern kitchen is sleek, clean &amp; functional</h2>

2945

2946

2947<p>

2948With these modern kitchen design ideas, you have plenty of options when it comes to transforming your kitchen into a modern masterpiece.</p>

2949

2950

2951<p>

2952Sticking to a neutral color palette of whites, grays, and blacks with a little pop of color, as well as focusing on straight vertical and horizontal lines, will do the trick to achieve a modern aesthetic.</p>

2953

2954

2955<p>

2956You can keep it simple by cleaning up the lines in the <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/kitchen-layout-ideas/" target="_blank">

2957kitchen layout</a>

2958 by replacing your cabinet doors, streamlining your hardware, or adding useful cabinet organization tools. Or you can go big and replace your cabinets, countertops, and other finishes in your kitchen to create a modern kitchen.</p>

2959

2960

2961<p>

2962If you&rsquo;d like guidance in modernizing your kitchen, Vevano Home designers would love to support you. Reach out today to see how you can elevate your kitchen to a modern style!</p>
